             </span>
             <div class="clear">
             </div>

             <div class="column-center-inner">
              <div class="main section" id="main">
               <div class="widget Blog" data-version="1" id="Blog1">
                <div class="blog-posts hfeed">
                 <div class="date-outer">
                  <h2 class="date-header">
                   <span>
                    Saturday, July 28, 2018
                   </span>
                  </h2>
                  <div class="date-posts">
                   <div class="post-outer">
                    <div class="post hentry">
                     <a name="835783767566153819">
                     </a>
                     <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                      <a href="http://veganfeastkitchen.blogspot.com/2018/07/moist-delicious-low-glycemicno-added.html">
                       MOIST &amp; DELICIOUS LOW-GLYCEMIC/NO-ADDED-SUGAR CORN MUFFINS
                      </a>
                     </h3>
                     <div class="post-header">
                      <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      </div>
                      <div id="fb-root">
                      </div>
                      <script src="http://connect.facebook.net/en_US/all.js#xfbml=1">
                      </script>
                      <fb:like href="http://veganfeastkitchen.blogspot.com/2018/07/moist-delicious-low-glycemicno-added.html" send="true" show_faces="false" width="450">
                      </fb:like>
                      <a href="http://www.spiceupyourblog.com">
                       <img alt="Best Blog Tips" src="http://img1.blogblog.com/img/blank.gif"/>
                      </a>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-DRM3dz4dxQU/W1v6OB3fo_I/AAAAAAAAJWM/j-DyBxfEn8skRY-kJpIfaTCx_8B1DYsTQCLcBGAs/s1600/Creamy%2BLG%2B%2Bcorn%2Bmuffins%2B%25281%2529.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" data-original-height="680" data-original-width="907" height="298" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-DRM3dz4dxQU/W1v6OB3fo_I/AAAAAAAAJWM/j-DyBxfEn8skRY-kJpIfaTCx_8B1DYsTQCLcBGAs/s400/Creamy%2BLG%2B%2Bcorn%2Bmuffins%2B%25281%2529.JPG" width="400"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <b style='font-family: Georgia, "Times New Roman", serif;'>
                       <br/>
                      </b>
                      <b style='font-family: Georgia, "Times New Roman", serif;'>
                       <br/>
                      </b>
                      <b style='font-family: Georgia, "Times New Roman", serif;'>
                       <br/>
                      </b>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <span style="color: black; text-align: start;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          As you might have noticed, I've been on vacation from blogging for almost a month. However, I haven't been idle.  You might remember me mentioning back in April that I was diagnosed as pre-diabetic, so I have been adjusting my vegan diet to a low-glycemic vegan diet, which means also adjusting some recipes, totally revamping others, or even starting from scratch, and tossing some out, as well.
                          <i>
                           (You can read a bit about this in
                          </i>
                          <a href="http://veganfeastkitchen.blogspot.ca/2018/03/why-i-havent-been-blogging-2-recipes.html" style="font-style: italic;">
                           this blog post
                          </a>
                          <i>
                           and
                          </i>
                          <a href="http://veganfeastkitchen.blogspot.com/2018/04/easy-bean-enhanced-vegan-burger-buns.html" style="font-style: italic;">
                           this one
                          </a>
                          <i>
                           . And, PS: I've dropped 13 lbs without even trying, and my blood tests are definitely improving. )
                          </i>
                          <br/>
                          <br/>
                          We mostly eat fresh fruit (often with homemade soy yogurt) when we want a dessert, but occasionally I make Chocolate "Nice Cream", made with 3 sliced frozen ripe bananas, 1/3 cup dark unsweetened cocoa powder, 1/4 cup soy milk, a pinch of salt, a little vanilla extract, and sometimes a dollop of nut butter, blended until creamy-smooth in the food processor, then frozen-- no sugar or sweetener of any kind needed! So delicious!
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <span style="color: black; text-align: start;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          <br/>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <span style="color: black; text-align: start;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          I've been eating only sprouted grain or whole rye breads, and also investigating other low-glycemic grains and flours. Quinoa, teff, and amaranth are all very well, but they are expensive (as is commercial sprouted grain flour), difficult for some people to find, and often too strong in taste to use in many recipes.
                          <span style="background-color: #f6b26b;">
                           My favorite quartet of LG flours
                          </span>
                          is comprised of oat flour, barley flour, millet flour (all can be ground from grain to flour in a dry high-speed blender if you do not have a grain mill) and
                          <span style='font-family: Georgia, "Times New Roman", serif; text-align: center;'>
                           chickpea flour. (White bean flour can be used in place of chickpea flour.) Buckwheat and rye are also excellent, and I always have some in my freezer, but their strong flavors make them less useful.
                          </span>
                          <br/>
                          <br/>
                          <span style='font-family: Georgia, "Times New Roman", serif; text-align: center;'>
                           Lately, I've been working on a low-glycemic, low-fat vegan brownie-- can you tell that we love chocolate? I'm not there yet, but will report back. Another recipe that
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia, "Times New Roman", serif; font-size: 16px;'>
                        I've been working on is a
                       </span>
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia, "Times New Roman", serif; font-size: 16px;'>
                       </span>
                       <span style='font-family: Georgia, "Times New Roman", serif; font-size: 12pt;'>
                        low-fat, but moist, low-glycemic vegan cornbread or corn muffin. Cornbread is a particular favorite of mine. I've tried many recipes from online sources and cookbooks, but, in the end I successfully revised one of my own corn muffin recipes and it's easy, quick, and inexpensive, as well as delicious.
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <span style="color: black; text-align: start;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          <span style='font-family: Georgia, "Times New Roman", serif; text-align: center;'>
                           <br/>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <span style="color: black; text-align: start;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          The following recipe is based on a recipe from my book
                          <i>
                           "The Fiber for Life Cookbook" (
                          </i>
                          Book Publishing Co., Summertown, TN; © 2002). It has
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <span style="text-align: start;">
                        <span style="font-family: georgia, serif; font-size: 12pt;">
                         been a favorite of ours for many years, because we love anything corn-y, and these are double-corn-y!
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: yellow; font-family: georgia, serif; font-size: 12pt;">
                         The canned cream-style corn in the recipe
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <span style="background-color: yellow; text-align: start;">
                        <i style="font-family: georgia, serif; font-size: 12pt;">
                         (which contains no cream or dairy whatsoever)
                        </i>
                        <span style="font-family: georgia, serif; font-size: 12pt;">
                         adds more fiber, and makes the muffins moist and sweet. If you don't have a can in your pantry, or prefer not to use it, you will need some thawed and drained frozen sweet corn-- see note at the end of the Ingredient List in the recipe.
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                        <b>
                         In this close-up,  you can see the nice moist crumb of the muffin.
                        </b>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Oqfw9nNxaz0/W1v8gQlg0nI/AAAAAAAAJWg/ezN8o5FIPD8DBfTAXhj1lURp_wN-iFV-gCLcBGAs/s1600/Creamy%2BLG%2B%2Bcorn%2Bmuffins%2B%25282%2529.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" data-original-height="680" data-original-width="907" height="298" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Oqfw9nNxaz0/W1v8gQlg0nI/AAAAAAAAJWg/ezN8o5FIPD8DBfTAXhj1lURp_wN-iFV-gCLcBGAs/s400/Creamy%2BLG%2B%2Bcorn%2Bmuffins%2B%25282%2529.JPG" width="400"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <b style='font-family: Georgia, "Times New Roman", serif;'>
                       <a href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/1xMCqYETtkgAApgT6fTC7k4-njrl0Pa2uMPttrXslqjw/">
                        Printable Recipe
                       </a>
                      </b>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <div style="break-before: page; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          <b>
                           BRYANNA'S
 MOIST &amp; DELICIOUS LOW-GLYCEMIC/NO-ADDED-SUGAR CORN MUFFINS
                           <br/>
                           Makes
 12
                          </b>
                          <br/>
                          <i>
                           <b>
                            (This recipe also happens to be gluten-free, can be soy-free, and contains no sugar or syrup of any kind, and no artificial sweeteners.)
                           </b>
                          </i>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          <i>
                           <b>
                            <br/>
                           </b>
                          </i>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <b style="font-family: georgia, serif; font-size: 12pt;">
                        DRY
 MIX:
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          1
 cup yellow cornmeal
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          1/2
 cup oat flour
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          1/4
 cup barley flour
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          1/4
 cup millet flour
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          1/2
 T. baking powder
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          1/2
 tsp. salt
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          1/4
 tsp. baking soda
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          <b>
                           WET
 MIX:
                          </b>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          3/4
 cup non-dairy milk
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          2
 T. oil
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          2
 tsp. powdered egg replacer
                          <i>
                           (such as Ener-G or Orgran)
                          </i>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          <b>
                           ADDITIONAL:
                          </b>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          14
 oz. can cream-style corn
                          <i>
                           <b>
                            (This product
 does NOT contain dairy products.)
                           </b>
                          </i>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <i style="font-family: georgia, serif;">
                        <b style="font-size: 12pt;">
                         OR,
                        </b>
                        <b>
                         in place of canned cream-style corn
                        </b>
                        <b style="font-size: 12pt;">
                         ,
                        </b>
                        <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                         you can mix 14 oz. of thawed frozen sweet corn (do not drain) with the Wet Mix ingredients in a blender or food processor for about 5 seconds-- some lumps of corn should remain. See photos below to judge texture.
                        </span>
                       </i>
                       <br/>
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          <i>
                           <b>
                            <br/>
                           </b>
                          </i>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                        <a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-QOSmPJp4GTA/W1ymB_XXM7I/AAAAAAAAJXA/JaS5v7TxkBYvNFxux19hGFHMvOORn7uwACLcBGAs/s1600/DelMonte_cream%2Bstyle%2Bcorn-crop.png" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                         <img border="0" data-original-height="329" data-original-width="486" height="270" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-QOSmPJp4GTA/W1ymB_XXM7I/AAAAAAAAJXA/JaS5v7TxkBYvNFxux19hGFHMvOORn7uwACLcBGAs/s400/DelMonte_cream%2Bstyle%2Bcorn-crop.png" width="400"/>
                        </a>
                       </div>
                       <br/>
                       <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                        <a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-FJNHus0cYDE/W1ymBb6WkxI/AAAAAAAAJW8/ee5a1Jp5KDgXkjFlam9ghyPA11ad6ilVQCLcBGAs/s1600/sweet-corn-cream-style-can-crop-crop.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                         <img border="0" data-original-height="442" data-original-width="707" height="250" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-FJNHus0cYDE/W1ymBb6WkxI/AAAAAAAAJW8/ee5a1Jp5KDgXkjFlam9ghyPA11ad6ilVQCLcBGAs/s400/sweet-corn-cream-style-can-crop-crop.jpg" width="400"/>
                        </a>
                       </div>
                       <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       </div>
                       <br/>
                       <b style="font-family: georgia, serif; font-size: 12pt;">
                        Instructions:
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          Preheat
 the oven to 375 degrees F.  Oil 12 muffin cups.   Mix
 the Dry Mix ingredients together well in a medium bowl.  Mix the
 Wet Mix ingredients in another (2 to 4-cup) bowl or pitcher with a
 whisk or with a hand/immersion blender.  Pour the contents of
 the can of "cream-style" corn into the Wet Mix and stir
 well.
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          Pour
 this mixture into the Dry Mix and mix briefly.  Spoon evenly
 into the muffin tin.  Bake 15-20 minutes.
                          <i>
                           (Test one of the muffins with a toothpick
 after 15 minutes, to see if the toothpick comes out clean--
                          </i>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <i>
                        <span style="font-family: georgia, serif; font-size: 16px;">
                         if it dies not,
                        </span>
                        <span style="font-family: georgia, serif; font-size: 12pt;">
                         bake for a few minutes more.).
                        </span>
                       </i>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          Loosen
 them carefully with a table knife and turn them on edge.  Place
 the muffin tin on a rack, cover the muffins with a clean tea towel
 and cool for a few minutes before serving.  Cool thoroughly
 before storing.  These freeze well.
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          <br/>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          <b>
                           Nutrition
 Facts
                          </b>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          <b>
                           Nutrition
 (per serving):
                          </b>
                          126 calories, 30 calories from fat, 3.4g total
 fat, 0mg cholesterol, 211.5mg sodium, 185.4mg potassium, 22.5g
 carbohydrates, 2.1g fiber, 1.6g sugar, 3g protein, 3.7 points.
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          Enjoy!
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          <br/>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm;">
                       <span style="color: black;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , serif;'>
                         <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                          <br/>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-VP0QUbItchs/W1v8dmwHCWI/AAAAAAAAJWk/dy1T6C2Q0eIN8D1gs2VAU-uhhGgig2yMQCEwYBhgL/s1600/tn_signature.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" data-original-height="76" data-original-width="200" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-VP0QUbItchs/W1v8dmwHCWI/AAAAAAAAJWk/dy1T6C2Q0eIN8D1gs2VAU-uhhGgig2yMQCEwYBhgL/s1600/tn_signature.jpg"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>

                      </div>

                 <div class="date-outer">
                  <h2 class="date-header">
                   <span>
                    Friday, June 1, 2018
                   </span>
                  </h2>
                  <div class="date-posts">
                   <div class="post-outer">
                    <div class="post hentry">
                     <a name="2873864569078929298">
                     </a>
                     <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                      <a href="http://veganfeastkitchen.blogspot.com/2018/06/easy-versatile-oat-okara-or-bean.html">
                       EASY, VERSATILE OAT &amp; OKARA-OR-BEAN-ENHANCED SEITAN CUTLETS
                      </a>
                     </h3>
                     <div class="post-header">
                      <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      </div>
                      <div id="fb-root">
                      </div>
                      <script src="http://connect.facebook.net/en_US/all.js#xfbml=1">
                      </script>
                      <fb:like href="http://veganfeastkitchen.blogspot.com/2018/06/easy-versatile-oat-okara-or-bean.html" send="true" show_faces="false" width="450">
                      </fb:like>
                      <a href="http://www.spiceupyourblog.com">
                       <img alt="Best Blog Tips" src="http://img1.blogblog.com/img/blank.gif"/>
                      </a>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-7YhdD3daDQ4/WxHp2UgCknI/AAAAAAAAJSg/hVVern6RAgwSjm8bL8igWlAPR-8mkjg2gCEwYBhgL/s1600/seared%2Bcutlet%2B%25284%2529.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" data-original-height="680" data-original-width="907" height="298" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-7YhdD3daDQ4/WxHp2UgCknI/AAAAAAAAJSg/hVVern6RAgwSjm8bL8igWlAPR-8mkjg2gCEwYBhgL/s400/seared%2Bcutlet%2B%25284%2529.JPG" width="400"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      </div>
                      <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                       This is my new favorite seitan recipe.  It's easy to make, has more fiber than most seitan, is tender and flavorful, a
                      </span>
                      <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                       nd is
                      </span>
                      <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                       very versatile.  The finished cutlets can be cut into cubes for stews and into strips for stir-fries.  I haven't tried this yet, but I think it would also make great sausages-- in fact, when my friend Tanya tasted this seitan in an Italian roasted stew (p. 172 in my vegan Italian cookbook,
                       <i>
                        <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Nonnas-Italian-Kitchen-Delicious-Home-Style/dp/1570670552">
                         "Nonna's Italian Kitchen"
                        </a>
                       </i>
                       ) that I made for a birthday potluck, she thought it was chunks of vegan Italian sausage!
                       <br/>
                       <br/>
                       <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                           <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                            <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                             <a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-4KRg64VOYuA/WxIH-MCybYI/AAAAAAAAJS0/lCEZURXPhJMxCJU-JDlWcYBPd2EGJDbMACEwYBhgL/s1600/Italian%2Broasted%2Bstew.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                              <img border="0" data-original-height="800" data-original-width="533" height="640" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-4KRg64VOYuA/WxIH-MCybYI/AAAAAAAAJS0/lCEZURXPhJMxCJU-JDlWcYBPd2EGJDbMACEwYBhgL/s640/Italian%2Broasted%2Bstew.jpg" width="425"/>
                             </a>
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <br/>
                          So that will be my next experiment, maybe with the addition of some different or additional  seasonings.  If it turns out well, I'll post about it, for sure.
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        <br/>
                        Enough said-- here's the recipe!
                        <br/>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="float: left; margin-right: 1em; text-align: left;">
                        <tbody>
                         <tr>
                          <td style="text-align: center;">
                           <a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ThU6A-wCgVU/WxHpw9kZlLI/AAAAAAAAJSo/NFxAmfAe614AW3KcUhGbCnVwPOjrdlLLgCEwYBhgL/s1600/cooked%2Bokara%2Boat%2Bseitan%2Bcutlets%2B3.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                            <img border="0" data-original-height="583" data-original-width="778" height="298" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ThU6A-wCgVU/WxHpw9kZlLI/AAAAAAAAJSo/NFxAmfAe614AW3KcUhGbCnVwPOjrdlLLgCEwYBhgL/s400/cooked%2Bokara%2Boat%2Bseitan%2Bcutlets%2B3.JPG" width="400"/>
                           </a>
                          </td>
                         </tr>
                         <tr>
                          <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                           <b>
                            Cutlets ready to cook, or to cut up for stews or stir-fries
                           </b>
                          </td>
                         </tr>
                        </tbody>
                       </table>
                       <br/>
                       <br/>
                       <br/>
                       <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                        <tbody>
                         <tr>
                          <td style="text-align: center;">
                           <a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-8U0DSEO35hg/WxHp4RB9LkI/AAAAAAAAJSk/0_7LM-5915Q_Q9mu70hTlq0nuuacUfPFwCEwYBhgL/s1600/seared%2Bcutlet%2B%25286%2529.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                            <img border="0" data-original-height="680" data-original-width="907" height="298" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-8U0DSEO35hg/WxHp4RB9LkI/AAAAAAAAJSk/0_7LM-5915Q_Q9mu70hTlq0nuuacUfPFwCEwYBhgL/s400/seared%2Bcutlet%2B%25286%2529.JPG" width="400"/>
                           </a>
                          </td>
                         </tr>
                         <tr>
                          <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                           <b>
                            Cutlet coated with Seasoned Flour, browned in a little oil and served with vegan gravy and sauteed mushrooms and onion
                           </b>
                          </td>
                         </tr>
                        </tbody>
                       </table>
                       <b>
                        <a href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/1mO0vz2zCWMnRpi-M-86SY6Dfi4f9tgxcJ2x8OQwMgTg/">
                         Printable Copy
                        </a>
                       </b>
                       <br/>
                       <br/>
                       <b>
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         BRYANNA'S EASY, VERSATILE OAT &amp; OKARA-OR-BEAN-ENHANCED SEITAN CUTLETS
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <br/>
                       <b>
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         Servings: 9
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <br/>
                       <b>
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         Yield: Makes 9/ 4 oz cutlets, or 36 oz. of seitan in total
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <br/>
                       <b>
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         <br/>
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        I usually make 3 times this recipe
                        <i>
                         (makes 27 cutlets-- see below for 3 x the recipe)
                        </i>
                        and freeze them.  They can be used as cutlets for a quick meal, or they can be cut into chunks for stews, or into slices for stir-fries and sautéed dishes, etc.
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        <br/>
                       </span>
                       <b>
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         Dry Mix:
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1 1/2 cups vital wheat gluten
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1/2 cup quick oats
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1/4 cup nutritional yeast flakes
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1 tsp onion powder
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1 tsp garlic granules or powder
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1/2 tsp dried thyme or sage
                        <i>
                         (or a mixture)
                        </i>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <b>
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         Wet Mix:
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1 3/4 cups water
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1 Tbs vegan broth powder
                        <i>
                         (use a tasty one)
                        </i>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        2 Tbs soy sauce or tamari
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1 Tbs olive oil
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1 cup fresh
                        <i>
                         (or thawed frozen)
                        </i>
                        okara
                        <i>
                         (pulp from making soymilk or tofu)
                        </i>
                        OR mashed cooked or canned
                        <i>
                         (rinsed and well-drained)
                        </i>
                        white beans
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='background-color: yellow; font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        <b>
                         NOTE:
                        </b>
                        you could use other types of beans, if you wish.
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <b>
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         Cooking Broth:
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        2 1/4 cups water
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        4 tsp mushroom powder
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='background-color: #f6b26b; font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        <b>
                         NOTE:
                        </b>
                        I grind dry, stemmed Chinese black mushrooms or shiitake mushrooms in a dry blender to make the powder.
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        4  tsp tasty vegan broth powder
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        4 tsp soy sauce or tamari
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        4 tsp minced garlic
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1 Tbs ketchup
                        <i>
                         (can be an organic brand)
                        </i>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1 Tbs olive oil or dark sesame oil
                        <i>
                         (or a mixture)
                        </i>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1 tsp onion powder
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1/2 Tbs dried sage
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        1/4 to 1/3 tsp paprika
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        <br/>
                       </span>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        Mix the Dry Mix ingredients together in a medium-sized bowl.
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        <br/>
                       </span>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        Mix the Wet Mix ingredients together in a pitcher.  Pour into the Dry Mix and combine with a spoon.  Knead for a few minutes, until a cohesive dough results.  Cover and let it rest for 30 minutes.
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        <br/>
                       </span>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        In the meantime, mix your Broth ingredients in a large pot and bring to a boil. Turn the heat off and cover.
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        Remove the dough from the bowl and flatten it out into a more-or-less even rectangle.  Cut with a bench knife/dough scraper or a knife into 9 fairly even chunks.
                       </span>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        It's preferable to weigh the chunks, so, if you have a kitchen scale use that to make 4 oz. chunks.  If there is any dough left over after weighing, divide it evenly between the chunks and knead it in.
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <br/>
                       <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-el5QwoplKMY/WxHp5QhKTUI/AAAAAAAAJSs/vn56yMA4_GIm1RRv6V4t6g0S0naysdK8ACEwYBhgL/s1600/sized%2Bokara%2Boat%2Bseitan%2Bcutlet%2Bdough.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                           <img border="0" data-original-height="583" data-original-width="778" height="298" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-el5QwoplKMY/WxHp5QhKTUI/AAAAAAAAJSs/vn56yMA4_GIm1RRv6V4t6g0S0naysdK8ACEwYBhgL/s400/sized%2Bokara%2Boat%2Bseitan%2Bcutlet%2Bdough.JPG" width="400"/>
                          </a>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         <br/>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <b>
                           To form the cutlets,
                          </b>
                          pat out each chunk on a silicone mat or clean counter (dampen your hands with water) until you have a fairly thin rectangle. Fold it in half one way and in half the other way.  Pat it again to make a cutlet about 1/4" thick.  It doesn't have to be an even shape, but even thickness is preferable.
                         </span>
                         <br/>
                         <br/>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                           <tbody>
                            <tr>
                             <td style="text-align: center;">
                              <a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-cfNegbXsRQM/WxHpymGB-1I/AAAAAAAAJSc/iXhbXdVXSFIA_tOxYQ1Nq_FUzjTqt6u7ACEwYBhgL/s1600/folded%2Band%2Brefolded%2Bokara%2Boat%2Bseitan%2Bcutlets.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                               <img border="0" data-original-height="583" data-original-width="778" height="298" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-cfNegbXsRQM/WxHpymGB-1I/AAAAAAAAJSc/iXhbXdVXSFIA_tOxYQ1Nq_FUzjTqt6u7ACEwYBhgL/s400/folded%2Band%2Brefolded%2Bokara%2Boat%2Bseitan%2Bcutlets.JPG" width="400"/>
                              </a>
                             </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                             <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                              <span style="font-size: small;">
                               <b>
                                On the left is the cutlet before folding; on the right is after folding and patting out again.
                               </b>
                              </span>
                             </td>
                            </tr>
                           </tbody>
                          </table>
                          <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                           <tbody>
                            <tr>
                             <td style="text-align: center;">
                              <a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-EyCkNxDSY5s/WxHp4R5_Q1I/AAAAAAAAJSo/a4PKdJkbrxYPVZsdtQy7LXGZ05T0tyZgACEwYBhgL/s1600/simmering%2Bokara%2Boat%2Bseitan%2Bcutlets.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                               <img border="0" data-original-height="583" data-original-width="778" height="298" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-EyCkNxDSY5s/WxHp4R5_Q1I/AAAAAAAAJSo/a4PKdJkbrxYPVZsdtQy7LXGZ05T0tyZgACEwYBhgL/s400/simmering%2Bokara%2Boat%2Bseitan%2Bcutlets.JPG" width="400"/>
                              </a>
                             </td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                             <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                              <b>
                               Simmered cutlets
                              </b>
                             </td>
                            </tr>
                           </tbody>
                          </table>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                           <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                            <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                             <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                              Bring the Broth to a boil and slip the cutlets into the Broth one at a time.  It's okay if they overlap a bit and if you have more than one layer.  Turn the heat down to Low, cover and simmer for 30 minutes. Turn off the heat, uncover and let it cool for a bit.
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <br/>
                         </span>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          Carefully remove from the pot-- you may have to use a small spatula or table knife to gently pry some of them apart.
                         </span>
                         <br/>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <br/>
                         </span>
                         <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                          <tbody>
                           <tr>
                            <td style="text-align: center;">
                             <a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-bj3uxTcA8gY/WxHpwunUmJI/AAAAAAAAJSg/zKumf8fO2R0Ri5Y4waZZ-Vayxyqk4HPmQCEwYBhgL/s1600/cooked%2Bokara%2Boat%2Bseitan%2Bcutlets%2B1.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                              <img border="0" data-original-height="583" data-original-width="778" height="298" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-bj3uxTcA8gY/WxHpwunUmJI/AAAAAAAAJSg/zKumf8fO2R0Ri5Y4waZZ-Vayxyqk4HPmQCEwYBhgL/s400/cooked%2Bokara%2Boat%2Bseitan%2Bcutlets%2B1.JPG" width="400"/>
                             </a>
                            </td>
                           </tr>
                           <tr>
                            <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                             <b>
                              Finished cutlets
                             </b>
                            </td>
                           </tr>
                          </tbody>
                         </table>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          Store in single layers between sheets of baking parchment in a large, flat freezer container with a tight lid.
                         </span>
                         <br/>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <br/>
                         </span>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          These will keep for about a week in the refrigerator, or for several months in the freezer.
                         </span>
                         <br/>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <br/>
                         </span>
                         <b>
                          <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                           To cook and serve the cutlets:
                          </span>
                         </b>
                         <br/>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <br/>
                         </span>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          You can coat the fresh or thawed-out cutlets in Seasoned Flour
                          <i>
                           (see below for recipe)
                          </i>
                          and sauté in a little oil in a heavy frying pan until golden and crunchy on both sides, OR coat with Seasoned Flour, then dip in soy or hemp milk that has been tcurdled to thicken by adding a bit of lemon juice (so that it's like buttermilk), then coated with whole grain dried breadcrumbs, such as whole wheat panko breadcrumbs.  Shallow-fry in a frying pan until golden and crunchy, or air-fry.  Serve either way with a sauce of your liking, or plain with your favorite accompaniment.
                         </span>
                         <br/>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <br/>
                         </span>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          The cutlets can also be cut into chunks and sautéed briefly to use in a stew.  They can also be cut into slices for stir-fries, or into thinner pieces (cut horizontally) for scallopine, sautéed and cooked in a sauce.
                         </span>
                         <br/>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <br/>
                         </span>
                         <b>
                          <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                           Nutrition Facts
                          </span>
                         </b>
                         <br/>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <b>
                           Nutrition (per cutlet):
                          </b>
                          158 calories, 21 calories from fat, 2.5g total fat, 0mg cholesterol, 366.9mg sodium, 261.3mg potassium, 15.1g carbohydrates, 3g fiber, 1g sugar, 20.5g protein, 4.2 points.
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <div>
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                        </span>
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <br/>
                          <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                           <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                            <b>
                             ADDITIONAL INFO:
                            </b>
                            <br/>
                            <span style="background-color: yellow;">
                             <br/>
                             <b style="background-color: yellow; font-weight: bold;">
                              <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                               FOR 3 TIMES THE RECIPE (108 OZ. OR 27/ 4 OZ CUTLETS):
                              </span>
                             </b>
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                        <br/>
                        <div>
                         <br/>
                         <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                          <b>
                           Dry Mix:
                          </b>
                         </span>
                        </div>
                        <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                         <span style='font-family: "georgia" , "times new roman" , serif;'>
                          <span style="background-color: yellow;">
                           <div>
                            4 1/2 cups vital wheat gluten
                            <br/>
                            1 1/2 cups quick oats
                            <br/>
                            3/4 cup nutritional yeast flakes
                            <br/>
                            1 Tbs. onion powder
                            <br/>
                            1 Tbs. garlic granules or powder
                            <br/>
                            1/2 Tbs. dried thyme or sage (or a mixture)
                            <br/>
                            <b>
                             Wet Mix:
                            </b>
                            <br/>
                            5 1/4 cups water
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            3 Tbs. vegan broth powder
                            <i>
                             (use a tasty one)
                            </i>
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            6 Tbsp. soy sauce or tamari
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            3 Tbsp. olive oil
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            3 cups fresh (or thawed frozen) okara
                            <i>
                             (pulp from making soymilk or tofu) OR mashed cooked or canned (rinsed and well-drained)
                            </i>
                            white beans
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            <b>
                             NOTE:
                             <i>
                              you could use other types of beans, if you wish.
                             </i>
                            </b>
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            <b>
                             Cooking Broth:
                            </b>
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            7 cups water
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            1/4 cup mushroom powder
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            <b>
                             NOTE:
                             <i>
                              I grind dry, stemmed Chinese black mushrooms or shiitake mushrooms in a dry blender to make the powder.
                             </i>
                            </b>
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            1/4 cup tasty vegan broth powder
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            1/4 cup soy sauce or tamari
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            1/4 cup minced garlic
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            3 Tbsp. ketchup
                            <i>
                             (can be an organic brand)
                            </i>
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            3 Tbsp. olive oil or dark sesame oil
                            <i>
                             (or a mixture)
                            </i>
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            1 Tbsp. onion powder
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            1/2 Tbsp. dried sage
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            3/4-1 tsp. paprika
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            <br/>
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            Proceed as directed in main recipe (use a large bowl), making 27/ 4 oz. cutlets. Cook in 2 large pots, each with a metal rack at the bottom of the pot.
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            <br/>
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            <b>
                             SEASONED FLOUR FOR DREDGING CUTLETS IF THEY ARE PLAIN, UN-COATED:
                            </b>
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            <b>
                             <i>
                              (This mixture is also useful for coating tofu, tempeh and seitan before pan-frying or broiling.)
                             </i>
                            </b>
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            <br/>
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            2 cups whole wheat flour
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            1/4 cup nutritional yeast flakes
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            1 tsp salt
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            1 tsp onion powder
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            OPTIONAL:
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            1 tsp garlic granules or powder
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            1 tsp paprika or smoked paprika
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            <br/>
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            Mix well and store in a tightly-covered container in your pantry.
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            <br/>
                           </div>
                           <div>
                            <div>
                             Enjoy!
                            </div>
                            <br/>
                            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; font-weight: bold; text-align: center;">
                             <a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-L4-aYJ5esas/WxHp-oPCEvI/AAAAAAAAJSQ/sjnhmYD8hxcI3qbh3WSbdGMQgTZ9poUSQCEwYBhgL/s1600/tn_signature.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                              <img border="0" data-original-height="76" data-original-width="200" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-L4-aYJ5esas/WxHp-oPCEvI/AAAAAAAAJSQ/sjnhmYD8hxcI3qbh3WSbdGMQgTZ9poUSQCEwYBhgL/s1600/tn_signature.jpg"/>
                             </a>
                            </div>
                            <br/>
                           </div>
                          </span>
                         </span>
