                 <div class="date-outer">
                  <h2 class="date-header">
                   <span>
                    Thursday, March 22, 2018
                   </span>
                  </h2>
                  <div class="date-posts">
                   <div class="post-outer">
                    <div class="post hentry">
                     <a name="563336958254717165">
                     </a>
                     <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                      <a href="http://veganfeastkitchen.blogspot.com/2018/03/cheese-y-charred-corn-green-bean-salad.html">
                       CHEESE-Y CHARRED CORN &amp; GREEN BEAN SALAD WITH GRAPE TOMATOES
                      </a>
                     </h3>
                     <div class="post-header">
                      <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      </div>
                      <div id="fb-root">
                      </div>
                      <script src="http://connect.facebook.net/en_US/all.js#xfbml=1">
                      </script>
                      <fb:like href="http://veganfeastkitchen.blogspot.com/2018/03/cheese-y-charred-corn-green-bean-salad.html" send="true" show_faces="false" width="450">
                      </fb:like>
                      <a href="http://www.spiceupyourblog.com">
                       <img alt="Best Blog Tips" src="http://img1.blogblog.com/img/blank.gif"/>
                      </a>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-DI9N_R0scmk/WrPzCFMHPCI/AAAAAAAAJAg/E1VxKTRVVvEC43DfA0Mx6lat52p6xgkIgCLcBGAs/s1600/Corn%2Btomato%2Band%2Bgreen%2Bbean%2Bsalad%2B%25281%2529.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" data-original-height="680" data-original-width="907" height="298" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-DI9N_R0scmk/WrPzCFMHPCI/AAAAAAAAJAg/E1VxKTRVVvEC43DfA0Mx6lat52p6xgkIgCLcBGAs/s400/Corn%2Btomato%2Band%2Bgreen%2Bbean%2Bsalad%2B%25281%2529.JPG" width="400"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       It's not so nice out now, but last week we had some sunny, warmish days-- enough to make me think of making a hearty salad for lunch instead of a soup.  It was almost shopping day, so I studied the contents of my refrigerator and freezer for what needed using and/or what was available, colorful and tasty.  I already had some of my staple low-fat balsamic vinaigrette made (see recipe below), so I kept that in mind as well.
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      So, here's what I came up with on short notice. It was easy to throw together and a hit with my husband (and also fed us for two lunches).  I hope you will enjoy it as much as we did!
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-zs78zkpMhYI/WrPzJAVw1pI/AAAAAAAAJA4/WsmfkeHYGi4o3vkVeho7DCbFljV5SpCnACEwYBhgL/s1600/Corn%2Btomato%2Band%2Bgreen%2Bbean%2Bsalad-crop.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" data-original-height="1242" data-original-width="1600" height="310" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-zs78zkpMhYI/WrPzJAVw1pI/AAAAAAAAJA4/WsmfkeHYGi4o3vkVeho7DCbFljV5SpCnACEwYBhgL/s400/Corn%2Btomato%2Band%2Bgreen%2Bbean%2Bsalad-crop.JPG" width="400"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        <a href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/1H9MeOZ7SCPzER8YXHOrLvBwihKNF7IvfU-NOt2s4uWI/">
                         Printable Copy
                        </a>
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        <br/>
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        BRYANNA'S CHEESE-Y CHARRED CORN &amp; GREEN BEAN SALAD WITH GRAPE TOMATOES
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        <br/>
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        Serves 4
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        <br/>
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       1 lb. slender fresh young green beans
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       1 tablespoon dark sesame oil
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       1 medium onion (whatever kind you like-- I used a white one), chopped
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       1 cup fresh or thawed frozen sweet corn kernels
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       1 cup red grape tomatoes, sliced in half lengthwise
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       about 1/2 cup Low-Fat Balsamic Vinaigrette (recipe below) or similar type of vinaigrette
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       1/4 to 1/2 cup of your favorite vegan Parmesan substitute (I used EarthIsland/FollowYour Heart)
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       Pick over the green beans, removing stems, and cook until tender, but not limp.  Cook them however you prefer-- they can be steamed, microwaved (in a tiny bit of water in a covered casserole), or brought to a boil just covered in water on the stove, then simmered for a few minutes, u ntil done to your liking.
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       Drain the beans in a colander and run cold water over them until they cool off a bit.  Leave in the colander to drain further.
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       Saute the onion in the sesame oil until they are softened and a little browned around the edges. set aside.
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       Spread the corn kernels on an oiled baking sheet and place about 4" under your oven's broiler.  Broil until they start to char a bit, toss them a bit with a spatula and mound them up a bit in the middle of the pan and broil for a few minutes more.  Set aside.
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       When everything is ready, toss the green beans, onion and corn together in a medium-sized serving bowl with the sliced grape tomatoes and salad dressing.  Divided between serving bowls and sprinkle each serving with some of the cheese.
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        Nutrition Facts
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        Nutrition (per serving):
                       </b>
                       204 calories, 34 calories from fat, 4g total fat, 0mg cholesterol, 172mg sodium, 458.7mg potassium, 29.9g carbohydrates, 5.8g fiber, 5.4g sugar, 8.3g protein, 5.2 points.
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       ****
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        BRYANNA'S BALSAMIC VINAIGRETTE
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        This is a good basic dressing for many types of salads.
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        Yield: 1 1/2 cups  S
                       </b>
                       <b>
                        ervings: 12
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        1 serving= 2 tablespoons
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       1  cup
                       <a href="http://veganfeastkitchen.blogspot.com/2007/05/lovely-spring-salad.html">
                        Fat-Free Oil Substitute for salad Dressings
                       </a>
                       OR aquafaba (unsalted chickpea broth from canned or home-cooked)
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       1/4 cup extra virgin olive oil
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       1/4 cup good-quality balsamic vinegar
                       <i>
                        (I prefer Costco's Kirkland  Signature brand, which is affordable, yet aged for 3 years and contains no wine vinegar or caramel color, unlike the 60-day-aged supermarket IGP brands.
                       </i>
                       <i>
                        See
                        <a href="http://www.costcoconnection.ca/connectioncaeng/20180506/?pg=89#pg89">
                         http://www.costcoconnection.ca/connectioncaeng/20180506/?pg=89#pg89
                        </a>
                       </i>
                       <i>
                        )
                       </i>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       1 tablespoon red wine vinegar
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       1 tablespoon Dijon mustard
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       1 tablespoon brown sugar
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       1 clove garlic, crushed
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       1 teaspoon salt
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       Whisk, shake, or blend the ingredients together well, bottle and store in the refrigerator.
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        Nutrition Facts
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        Nutrition (per serving):
                       </b>
                       50 calories, 40 calories from fat, 4.6g total fat, 0mg cholesterol, 175.5mg sodium, 12.9mg potassium, 2.6g carbohydrates, less than 1g fiber, 1.1g sugar, less than 1g protein, 1.5 points.
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Ou6UdyaXuPQ/WrPzCAPPllI/AAAAAAAAJAw/uOSmq4jrl5QGRTg3Tw5_-NYYFNeXRlgwwCEwYBhgL/s1600/Corn%2Btomato%2Band%2Bgreen%2Bbean%2Bsalad%2B%25282%2529.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" data-original-height="680" data-original-width="907" height="298" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Ou6UdyaXuPQ/WrPzCAPPllI/AAAAAAAAJAw/uOSmq4jrl5QGRTg3Tw5_-NYYFNeXRlgwwCEwYBhgL/s400/Corn%2Btomato%2Band%2Bgreen%2Bbean%2Bsalad%2B%25282%2529.JPG" width="400"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       Enjoy!
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-aBb-2SkMkh8/WrPzD3NYtcI/AAAAAAAAJA0/gSTr3qsSkWQrZKDYe5zjd-jgaRw8ZlgHgCEwYBhgL/s1600/tn_signature.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" data-original-height="76" data-original-width="200" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-aBb-2SkMkh8/WrPzD3NYtcI/AAAAAAAAJA0/gSTr3qsSkWQrZKDYe5zjd-jgaRw8ZlgHgCEwYBhgL/s1600/tn_signature.jpg"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <div style="clear: both;">
                      </div>
                     </div>

                  </a>

                <div class="widget Text" data-version="1" id="Text3">
                 <h2 class="title">
                  ABOUT MISSING PHOTOS ON OLDER BLOG POSTS:
                 </h2>
                 <div class="widget-content">
                  <div class="" data-block="true" data-editor="81fho" data-offset-key="57cpv-0-0" style='white-space: pre-wrap;font-family:";color#000000;'>
                   <div class="_1mf _1mj" data-offset-key="57cpv-0-0" style="direction: ltr; position: relative;font-family:inherit;">
                    <span style="font-size:;">
                     <span style="font-family;">
                      If you are wondering what happened to the photos on my older blog posts, here's the deal:  I used to use Photobucket to store my photos and uploaded them to my blog posts from there.  Since about 2012, I have uploaded pics from my computer files instead.  All of a sudden, Photobucket is demanding $39 a month for storage and you can't download pictures to blogs or other sites unless you pay that.  I find that fee outrageous (and I'm not the only one!). UPDATE: I discovered that I could upload albums from from PB to my computer (or external hard drive).  So, I have done that, but it took a couple of days.  Now I just have to locate the correct pictures for the old blogs! One step at a time. My apologies... please bear with me! BCG
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="clear">
                 </div>
                 <span class="widget-item-control">
                  <span class="item-control blog-admin">
                   <a class="quickedit" href="//www.blogger.com/rearrange?blogID=24141461&amp;widgetType=Text&amp;widgetId=Text3&amp;action=editWidget&amp;sectionId=sidebar-right-1" onclick='return _WidgetManager._PopupConfig(document.getElementById("Text3"));' target="configText3" title="Edit">
                    <img alt="" height="18" src="https://resources.blogblog.com/img/icon18_wrench_allbkg.png" width="18"/>
                   </a>
                  </span>

                    <div class="widget Text" data-version="1" id="Text2">
                     <h2 class="title">
                      I HAVEN'T HAD TIME TO CHANGE ALL MY RECIPES THAT CALL FOR VEGAN MARGARINE
                     </h2>
                     <div class="widget-content">
                      <span>
                       <span style="font-size:100%;">
                        I am slowly trying to update them. But I am now using my palm oil-free vegan
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <a href="http://veganfeastkitchen.blogspot.ca/p/introducing-homemade-palm-oil-free.html" style="font-family: Georgia, serif; font-size: 100%; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; ">
                       "Buttah"
                      </a>
                      <span>
                       <span style="font-size:100%;">
                        instead. (Just so you know I'm
                       </span>
                       practising
                       <span style="font-size:100%;">
                        what I preach.  I haven't bought margarine since December 2011.)
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="clear">
                     </div>
                     <span class="widget-item-control">
                      <span class="item-control blog-admin">
                       <a class="quickedit" href="//www.blogger.com/rearrange?blogID=24141461&amp;widgetType=Text&amp;widgetId=Text2&amp;action=editWidget&amp;sectionId=sidebar-right-2-1" onclick='return _WidgetManager._PopupConfig(document.getElementById("Text2"));' target="configText2" title="Edit">
                        <img alt="" height="18" src="https://resources.blogblog.com/img/icon18_wrench_allbkg.png" width="18"/>
                       </a>
                      </span>
                     </span>

                       </dt>
                       <dd class="profile-textblock">
                        Author of 8 published vegan cookbooks (and contributor to several others) including the new book, World Vegan Feast, published in August 2011 (Vegan Heritage Press). Vegan since 1988.  Bellydancing mother of 4, stepmother of 2, grandmother of 5 girls and 2 boys. 
 https://www.facebook.com/bryannaclark.grogan
 If you would like to share any of my recipes with others, or on a forum, or another site, let me know, and please credit me, my website or blog and the book the recipe appeared in, if I note that in the recipe. You are welcome to link to this page from your site. Thanks!
 CONTACT me at bryannaclark.grogan@facebook.com
 © Bryanna Clark Grogan
                       </dd>
                      </dl>
